 The US branch of Chinese company Huawei recently sued the US Ministry of Commerce in a regional court in Washington
 america-china ke bich jari trade war kaa khamiyaja huaave ko bhugatna pad rahaa he, kyonki america sarkaar ne us par bain laga diya he
 However, Huawei's case relates to an earlier case
 news agency ieenes ke mutabik, maamla saal 2017 kaa he
 The US Ministry of Commerce took possession of Huawei's equipment and did not take a long decision, which Huawei said was illegal
 adaalat main daakhil apil dastavej ke mutabik, saal 2017 main huaave ne computer sarwar samet kuch china main utpaadit doorsanchaar upkarnon ko jaanch ke liye california main ek swatantra prayogshaala main pahunchaaya
 These devices were to be repatriated after a planned investigation, but in September of that year, the US Ministry of Commerce investigated export permission on the way to return these devices to China and closed them in the anchorage city of Alaska State 
 apil dastavej main kaha gaya he ki upkarnon ko kabje main liye jane ke baad huaave ne maang ke anusaar sambandhit soochna pesh kii or suchit kiya gaya ki america vaanijya mantralay ke adheen sanstha aam taur par 45 dinon ke bheetar niryaat anumati se sambandhit faisla karegi
 It has been more than 20 months since the equipment was captured by the US, but the US Commerce Ministry still did not take a decision
 huaave kaa kahana he ki america ke baahar utpaadit upkarnon ko utpaadan desh main waapas pahunchane ke liye koi niryaat anumati kii aavashyaktaa nahin he
 Whether or not the US Ministry of Commerce's early possession of the equipment is wrong or not, its decision to unduly give it back is invalid
 huwave ne america vaanijya mantralay se sambandhit upkarnon ke parivahan main niyam kaa ulanghan karne yaa na karne par faisla karne kaa anurodh kiya
 If it is decided not to violate the rule, the US Ministry of Commerce should allow the equipment to be returned to China
 gauratlab he ki huaave ke america se rishte kuch thik nahin chal rahe
 The US government recently banned Chinese company Huawei and several of its units
 inamen china main registerd is samooh kii 35 companiyaan or huaave srilanka, huaave honkong, huaave pakistan shaamil hai
 The US government feels that the Chinese company Huawei is acting as an agent of the Chinese government to spy on the US and because of this, US President Donald Trump has taken tough measures against Huawei
 america main huaave ko bain karne ke baad Google ne huaave se android kaa license cancil kar diya tha
 Google had said that it had not canceled Android's license for Huawei by itself, but that Google was following the order of the US Commerce Department

 haalanki is company kaa 4G network philhal kuch sarkal main hi he

 That is, Telenor has launched this plan to compete with Reliance Jio at its level
 lekin jeeyo kaa aisa hi plan 303 rupee main aata he or har din 1jibi data yuj kiya ja saktaa he

 South Africa's captain Graeme Smith has announced that he will say goodbye to international cricket after the current third Test cricket match against Australia in Newlands
 antarrashtriya cricket main sabase adhik samay tak captain bane rahane kaa record rakhane vaale 33 varshiya smith ke lambey samay tak unke saathi rahe jaak kallis ne disambar main test cricket ko alavida kaha tha, lekin vah ekadivasiy team kaa hissaa bane hue hai
 Smith said on Friday that he still had some things to achieve in international cricket, but after another failure in the current series, he decided that the time had come to retire
 smith ne somvaar ko pehali pari main keval paanch ran banaae the
 He said here on Monday, 'this was the most difficult decision of my life
 pichley saal april main takhne ke oparation ke baad main is faisle par vichaar kar rahaa tha
 My children are young and i feel that retiring in Newlands is the best place to end my career because i have been calling this place my home since i was 18 years old
 ' Smith captained South Africa in 108 matches for over 11 years

 ) Google, Facebook and Twitter have come on one platform to prevent worldwide child sexual abuse on the Internet
 bal yon shoshan se jude photose ko internet se hataane or internet par fail rahe bal yon shoshan ko rokane ke liefesbuk, google or twitor britain kii charity internet vaach foundation ke saath milakar kaam kar raheen hai
 These companies are working on digital fingerprint technology through which any photo related to child sexual abuse will be removed as soon as it is posted on the Internet
 pichley dino britain ke pradhanmantri david camran ne yah elaan kiya tha ki britain kii suraksha agenciyaan unalogon ke khilaaf muhim chalaaengi jo bal yon shoshan kii photo or video kaa avaidh dhandha karte hai jise dark trade ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Internet companies are developing a system called 'hash'
 is system ke tahat agar koi bhi bal yon shoshan se juudi photo internet par aplod karegaa uski report khud internet vaach foundation par chali jaaegi phir internet vaach foundation internet companiyon ko us photo ko hataane kii requawst bhejkar use internet se remov kara degaa
 Although Internet companies have been using URL Blocking technology in the past to remove pornographic photos, but this system is considered more effective than that
 yah system us photo ko bhi remov kar degaa jise child abuger kai naamon se post karte hai
 According to Susie Hargrave, chief executive of the Internet Watch Foundation, the 'internet Watch Foundation hash technology' will serve as a game changer for growing child sexual exploitation on the Internet
 saath hi duniya bhar main fail rahe bal yon shoshan kii photo par rog lagaaegi

 cocaine dopamine kaa str badhaakar mastishk ko prabhavit karti he
 Dopamine is a brain transmitter that plays important roles in brain functioning
 in bhoomikaaon main sammaan evam anand kii anubhuti bhi shaamil he
 Cocaine inhibits proteins that absorb dopamine again
 isse dopamine paidaa hota jaataa he or vyakti ko ‘ucchtam’str par anand kii anubhuti hoti he
 Lead researcher Zhou Jiawei, a team from the Shanghai Institutes for Biological Sciences under the Chinese Academy of Sciences, said that during addiction, a protein called dopamine transporter (DAT) moves to the cell surface, accelerating the nerve cell
 tippaniyan Quoting Zhou, the official newspaper China Daily said, "we found that the state of DAT in the brain makes the major difference
" unhone kaha, ulat sthiti main yah sthanantaran nahin hoga or is tarah se lat badhane par roak lagaai ja sakati he
 The research team believes that the key to stopping addiction is hidden in a small protein called VAV2, which acts like a molecular switch, regulating the transfer of DAT
 vaigyanikon kaa kahana he ki viavi2 kii is bhoomika kii khoj kaa istemaal cocaine ke aadi logon ko sudhaarney ke prayaason main kiya ja saktaa he
